INC Number: INC0492379

Category: MASTERING

Team: T2

FAD Reason: This is functioning as designed. The box needs to be unchecked each time the instructor manages incompletes: https://help.pearsoncmg.com/xl/instructor/instructor_help/Content/submit_scores_incompletes.htm. If they would like to delete 0 scores that they did not mean to give to specific students, they can click on those scores in the gradebook, select the dropdown next to the assignment on the next page, and delete the 0 score. However, please caution them that deleting is permanent; therefore, they want to be careful when doing this to avoid deleting any actual scores.

Case Number: 50467926

Product Issue: Revel - Total points not changing even after editing the Global settings

INC Number: INC0495929

Category: MASTERING

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: This is FAD. The locked scoring policy for the assignment was set to 0. Once a student starts the assessment that scoring policy can not be changed. Changing the Global Scoring policy only makes changes to items that have not been engaged by a student and locked. To view the scoring policy you can edit the assignment > click the 3 dots next to the assessment > click view scoring policy.

Tags: PR_FAD, Scoring_Policy

Case Number: 50195850

Product Issue: MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

INC Number: INC0475294

Category: MASTERING

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

Tags: 3PL_1.3, 3PL_FAD, 3PL_GS

Case Number: 50558734

Product Issue: MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

INC Number: INC0500673

Category: MASTERING

Team: T3

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Case Number: 50195850

Product Issue: MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

INC Number: INC0475294

Category: MMND

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

Case Number: 50558734

Product Issue: MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

INC Number: INC0500673

Category: MMND

Team: T3

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Case Number: 50467926

Product Issue: Revel - Total points not changing even after editing the Global settings

INC Number: INC0495929

Category: REVEL

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: This is FAD. The locked scoring policy for the assignment was set to 0. Once a student starts the assessment that scoring policy can not be changed. Case Number: 50195850

Product Issue: MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

INC Number: INC0475294

Category: REVEL

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

As this still has "status" : "RECEIVED", meaning it hasn't been delivered, I checked the gradeSetting collection; which has the sync details, and can see that this is set to automatic, but specific assignments. The list doesn't include the assignments they have mentioned are missing from the LMS gradebook. Please work with the instructor to select the assignments they wish to sync from the instructor dashboard > grade sync tab and then run the manual grade sync.

Case Number: 50558734

Product Issue: MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

INC Number: INC0500673

Category: REVEL

Team: T3

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Case Number: 50467926

Product Issue: Revel - Total points not changing even after editing the Global settings

INC Number: INC0495929

Category: XL

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: This is FAD. The locked scoring policy for the assignment was set to 0. Once a student starts the assessment that scoring policy can not be changed. Changing the Global Scoring policy only makes changes to items that have not been engaged by a student and locked. To view the scoring policy you can edit the assignment > click the 3 dots next to the assessment > click view scoring policy.

Case Number: 50195850

Product Issue: MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

INC Number: INC0475294

Category: XL

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

Case Number: 50558734

Product Issue: MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

INC Number: INC0500673

Category: XL

Team: T3

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Product Issue: Revel - Total points not changing even after editing the Global settings

INC Number: INC0495929

Category: REGISTRATION

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: This is FAD. The locked scoring policy for the assignment was set to 0. Once a student starts the assessment that scoring policy can not be changed. To view the scoring policy you can edit the assignment > click the 3 dots next to the assessment > click view scoring policy.

Case Number: 50195850

Product Issue: MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

INC Number: INC0475294

Category: REGISTRATION

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

Case Number: 50558734

Product Issue: MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

INC Number: INC0500673

Category: REGISTRATION

Team: T3

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Product Issue: Revel - Total points not changing even after editing the Global settings

INC Number: INC0495929

Category: PEARSON+

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: This is FAD. The locked scoring policy for the assignment was set to 0. Once a student starts the assessment that scoring policy can not be changed. Changing the Global Scoring policy only makes changes to items that have not been engaged by a student and locked. To view the scoring policy you can edit the assignment > click the 3 dots next to the assessment > click view scoring policy.

Case Number: N/A

Product Issue: MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

INC Number: INC0475294

Category: PEARSON+

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

Case Number: N/A

Product Issue: MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

INC Number: INC0500673

Category: PEARSON+

Team: T3

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Case Number: 50652759

INC Number: INC0510407

Category: Additional FAD cases

Team: Frezalin Bascara

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Support this is FAD. This is straight from the help file so please make sure you're doing your due diligence before sending something up to engineering. https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=revel-glp-instructor&topicId=Content/6-settings/how-settings-work.htm&_LANG=enus Unlimited tries If your course includes questions, such as code questions, with an unlimited number of possible answers, and you select the Unlimited tries option, students can answer the question as many times as they choose. If, however, you select unlimited tries for assessments with questions that have a set number of answers, Revel limits the tries to the number of answers minus 1, as described above.

Category: Additional FAD cases

In regards to the Learning Aid changes - these can only be changed on assignments that students have not started. Please let me know if you have any questions.

Case Number: 50723660

Product Issue: Mastering Biology - Student Late Penalty

INC Number: INC0518679

Category: Additional FAD cases

Team: N/A

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: This is expected behavior in Mastering Platform Update. The original due date for the assignment was September 24th; however, the instructor applied individual student settings to the assignment (I suspect after the student completed it) to give this student a due date October 3rd. Unlike legacy Mastering, Mastering Platform Update does not automatically regrade student submissions when a new due date is applied. For the new settings to apply to the student's submission, the student needs to reopen the assignment. Since the new due date has passed, the instructor will need to push it out to any time in the future, and then the student will need to reopen and save the assignment before the new due date passes.

Tags: incorrect_score, MX_MPU, PR_FAD

Category: INFO

Team: T3

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Hi Melissa, Now that Auto Grade sync is turned on this should let the grades sync right when they are completed by the student and should also stop these "false" late submissions that are only showing on the Canvas side as the grade is showing up correctly on the Revel side. Unfortunately to my knowledge there is no way to retroactively fix the Canvas gradebook but that would be a question for the school Canvas admin or Canvas support. If this is still happening on future assignments that haven't been completed yet and the grades sync automatically please give us one student and the exercise so that we can look into this. The Revel and Learning Management System team are aware that submission time aren't sent to the LMS and the sync time is what is view by the Learning Management System as the "submit time" and can cause this issue. Unfortunately I do not have an ETA on when this will be changed but it is something the teams are working diligently on.

Case Number: N/A

Product Issue: MyLab Math - Grades not syncing

INC Number: INC0475294

Category: Team Frez HETS INFO_FAD Aug19to

Team: T2

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: #FAD - assignments are set to 'omit results' in XL course, so are not sent to LMS. In XL, there are two settings that control the sending of assignments and grades to the LMS, 1) Grade Sync Settings - This is where the instructor can set to sync grades to the LMS 2) Change Weights and Categories - Any assignments set to 'omit' will not send to the LMS. Please make sure you are checking both these locations in your investigation.

The list doesn't include the assignments they have mentioned are missing from the LMS gradebook. Please work with the instructor to select the assignments they wish to sync from the instructor dashboard > grade sync tab and then run the manual grade sync.

Case Number: N/A

Product Issue: MPU - Interactive Reading and DSM assigment (attempts not working)

INC Number: INC0500673

Category: Team Frez HETS INFO_FAD Aug19to

Team: T3

FAD Reason: N/A

Resolution Notes: Hi Michael, It sounds like there is some confusion between tries and attempts here. The students are getting two tries and 10 attempts. Each time they click the check answer or final check button, that counts as a try. When they click try again, that counts as a new attempt, so they get two tries to answer the questions with each of the 10 attempts the instructor has provided. You can learn more by reviewing this help file: https://support.pearson.com/getsupport/s/document-item?bundleId=Tries-vs-attempts-in-MyLab-and-Mastering&topicId=Tries_vs_Attempts.html&_LANG=enus.

Tags: MX_MPU, PR_FAD
